I finally gave up on the cordless models, purchased a Trimmit Nose Hair Trimmer and settled for Platinum XL Nose Hair Trimmer for the past 5 years. This last one works well if I am careful to turn the end as I push the cutting tip into my nose, but because the motor is your fingers turning the end, I must stop pushing it further into my nose while I'm winding up my hand to spin the tail again. If I forget to stop pushing it into my nose when I'm not turning the end, the trimmer then acts like a massive needle nose pliers and painfully yanks on the hairs in my nose. It also requires the use of two hands and is a slow process.   585. While I wouldn't say I have a forest of hair in my nostrils, I have noticed that several individual hairs have transgressed a length that would be considered proper by men's grooming standards. So, naturally when I know what I want, but not exactly which product, I head to the world's largest marketplace, Amazon. This particular nose-hair trimmer was well reviewed. The features many users liked were the metal handle and the solid build quality. I will agree, this is comfortable to hold and is feels well made.<br /><br />During operation, the trimmer technology operates like a dry-shave electric razor, like Norelco or Panasonic branded ones. It spins around blades at high RPMs while a slotted (perforated) metal tip, the part of the trimmer that looks like a bullet jacket, gets your hairs stuck inside the little holes to then be cut by the spinning blade. This technique allows for convenient operation; however, you have to run it for at least a minute or two to get decent nose-hair cutting to result. Because, the nose hairs have to enter the small holes in the tip in order to be cut - this is something that cannot be controlled so you have to keep moving the trimmer around your nose quite a bit. While being used in this manner, the motor's energy transmitted to the spinning blade tends to make the slotted tip quite hot to touch - and you can feel it get hot in your nostril. In conclusion, it works. It's decently made and it is very simple to use and clean. It is not very efficient at cutting hairs and can get hot enough during use that you have to stop operation to let it cool down. It is a tad bit more expensive than some other nose hair trimmers that seem to have a lot more frills and features. It does remove hair with time - and heat - though I was hoping it would be more effective at removing hair so it would take less time.
